# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

**Task ID**: csharp_ml_training_expert_087_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Task Title

Architectural Refactoring: Decompose Monitoring Module into a Microservice

## Description

CanvasCraft ML Studio is currently architected as a C# modular monolith. A key business requirement has emerged to scale the model monitoring capabilities independently from the core application. The `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` module, which is responsible for detecting data drift and performance degradation in deployed models, has been identified as a prime candidate for extraction into a separate microservice. This task requires the agent to analyze the existing architecture and formulate a detailed plan for this decomposition.

## Your Task

You are a senior software architect. Your task is to create a detailed architectural refactoring plan to extract the `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` project into a new, standalone microservice. Your plan must be based on a thorough analysis of the existing codebase and architectural documents.

Your final output should be a technical plan that addresses the following points:

1.  **Analysis of Current State:** Briefly describe how the monitoring system currently works within the modular monolith. Identify the key components involved and their interaction patterns (e.g., how monitoring is triggered and how its results are consumed).

2.  **Proposed Microservice Architecture:**
    a.  **Communication Strategy:** Define how the new `MonitoringService` will communicate with the main `CanvasCraft.Api` application. Justify your choice of communication pattern (e.g., synchronous vs. asynchronous) by referencing existing patterns in the codebase.
    b.  **Data Flow:** Detail the flow of data and events between the main application and the new microservice. Specifically, explain what triggers the monitoring logic and how the results (e.g., a detected drift) are communicated back to the system to trigger actions like automated retraining.

3.  **Implementation & Refactoring Plan:**
    a.  **Code Changes:** List the primary projects and specific files/classes in the existing solution that will require modification. Describe the nature of the changes needed (e.g., removal of code, modification of a service client).
    b.  **New Components:** Describe the high-level structure of the new `MonitoringService`, including its API contract if it requires one.
    c.  **Deployment:** Explain how the `docker-compose.yml` file should be updated to include the new microservice for local development and testing.

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would approach this task by first building a mental model of the system, synthesizing information from both documentation and code.

1.  **Documentation Review:** The developer would start by reading the architecture documents, specifically `docs/architecture/adr/001-modular-monolith-architecture.md` and `docs/architecture/adr/002-event-driven-monitoring.md`. This provides the high-level context that the system is intentionally designed as a modular monolith and uses event-driven patterns for decoupling.

2.  **Code Analysis - Triggering Monitoring:** The developer would trace the execution path for model predictions. They would look at `CanvasCraft.Api/Controllers/ServingController.cs` to see how predictions are handled. They would likely find that it publishes an event, such as `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent`, onto a message bus.

3.  **Code Analysis - Monitoring Logic:** Next, they would examine the `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` project. They'd identify that it uses an Observer pattern (`IModelObserver`, `ModelServingSubject`) and is likely running as a background service within the main monolith, subscribing to the events published by the API via `IMessageBus` (implemented by `RabbitMqService.cs`). The observers (`DataDriftObserver`, `PerformanceFadeObserver`) contain the core detection logic.

4.  **Code Analysis - Consuming Results:** The developer would investigate how monitoring results are used. They would find the `CanvasCraft.Pipeline/Triggers/AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs` and determine how it's activated. It's likely that the observers, upon detecting an issue, publish a *new* event (e.g., `DriftDetectedEvent`, `RetrainingRequiredEvent`) to the message bus, which the `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` subscribes to.

5.  **Formulating the Plan:** Based on this analysis, the developer would formulate the plan:
    *   Propose that the new microservice will contain the code from the `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` project.
    *   Confirm that the communication should remain asynchronous using the existing RabbitMQ infrastructure to maintain loose coupling, as established in the ADRs.
    *   The main API's responsibility remains unchanged: publish prediction events.
    *   The new `MonitoringService` will be the sole subscriber to these prediction events.
    *   The `MonitoringService`, upon detecting an issue, will publish a `RetrainingRequiredEvent` (or similar) back to RabbitMQ.
    *   The `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` in the main application's `Pipeline` module will remain, but its subscription logic will now listen for events from the external service rather than an in-process source.
    *   The `docker-compose.yml` file will be modified to add a new service definition for the `monitoring-service`, configuring its build context, network, and environment variables (e.g., RabbitMQ connection string).
    *   Identify that `CanvasCraft.Api/Startup.cs` will need to be cleaned up to remove the DI registration for the monitoring observers.

## Evaluation Criteria

- Correctly identifies the existing architecture as a modular monolith with event-driven communication via RabbitMQ.
- Accurately describes the current data flow from API event publication to monitoring consumption and subsequent trigger activation.
- Proposes a viable, asynchronous communication pattern for the new microservice that leverages existing infrastructure (RabbitMQ).
- Clearly defines the responsibilities of both the main application and the new microservice in the proposed architecture.
- Correctly identifies the full-circle event path, including how monitoring results are communicated back to trigger retraining.
- Lists the key files/areas for modification, including `Startup.cs` (DI removal), project references, and `docker-compose.yml`.
- Demonstrates an understanding of microservice principles by creating a plan that promotes loose coupling and independent deployment.

     2→Status: Accepted  
     3→Date: 2024-06-08  
     4→Deciders: Core Architecture Working Group (CAWG)  
     5→Supersedes: *n/a*

     8→---
     9→
    10→## 1. Context  
    11→
    12→CanvasCraft ML Studio is an end-to-end **MVC-driven MLOps platform** that targets creative professionals iterating on generative media.  
    13→While the business road-map forecasts multiple deployment targets (desktop, on-prem, cloud, edge), the immediate product goals are:
    14→
    15→* Rapid iteration on **feature-engineering palettes** and **hyper-parameter color-wheels**.  
    16→* Tight coupling between **experiment-tracking**, **feature store**, and **model registry** to guarantee lineage.  
    17→* A **reactive model-monitoring** feedback loop that must not fall out of sync with training pipelines.  
    18→* A single deployable artifact that remains **operationally simple** yet **modular enough** to allow multiple teams (Data Science, UX, DevOps) to collaborate in parallel.
    19→
    20→The team evaluated the following architectural styles:
    21→
    22→| Candidate | Pros | Cons |
    23→|-----------|------|------|
    24→| Pure Micro-services | Independent deployability; granular scaling | YAGNI for current size; high operational overhead; transaction boundaries complicate ACID model registry |
    25→| **Modular Monolith (Internal Hexagons)** | Clear module boundaries; performant in-process calls; single deployment unit | Requires discipline to avoid “big ball of mud”; limited horizontal scaling |
    26→| Packaged Plugins (OSGi style) | Hot-swappable “brush” plugins; strict contracts | Added complexity to load/

    17→
    18→## 1. Context  
    19→
    20→CanvasCraft ML Studio serves creative professionals who demand instant
    21→feedback when a model’s aesthetic *or* quantitative performance drifts.
    22→Traditional, pull-based dashboards proved too latent for interactive
    23→workflows. We therefore require:
    24→
    25→* Near-real-time detection of data and model drift  
    26→* Reactive alerting to UI canvases, Slack, and WebHooks  
    27→* Loose coupling between producers (model training, feature store) and
    28→  consumers (dashboards, alerting services, auto-retrain jobs)  
    29→* A pluggable architecture that works in single-process testbeds **and**
    30→  distributed production clusters  
    31→
    32→These constraints map naturally to an **Event-Driven Architecture (EDA)**
    33→implemented via the **Observer Pattern**.
    34→
    35→---
    36→
    37→## 2. Decision  
    38→
    39→We will implement a lightweight, in-process **Event Bus** backed by
    40→`System.Threading.Channels` for default deployments, with adapters that
    41→proxy to external brokers (Kafka / Azure Event Hubs) for scale-out
    42→environments. All monitoring signals will be published as immutable
    43→domain events implementing `IMod

     1→```csharp
     2→using System;
     3→using System.Collections.Generic;
     4→using System.Net.Mime;
     5→using System.Text.Json;
     6→using System.Text.Json.Serialization;
     7→using System.Threading;
     8→using System.Threading.Tasks;
     9→using CanvasCraft.Domain.Exceptions;
    10→using CanvasCraft.Domain.Inferencing;
    11→using CanvasCraft.Domain.ModelRegistry;
    12→using CanvasCraft.Domain.Tracking;
    13→using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http;
    14→using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;

    16→
    17→namespace CanvasCraft.Api.Controllers
    18→{
    19→    /// <summary>
    20→    ///     ReST controller responsible for runtime model serving.  
    21→    ///     Provides prediction, metadata lookup and live-reload endpoints.
    22→    /// </summary>

     1→```markdown
     2→# CanvasCraft ML Studio – Architecture Overview
     3→*Project: `ml_training` • Language: C# (.NET 8) • Pattern Palette: MVC, MLOps Pipeline, Strategy, Factory, Observer*
     4→
     5→---
     6→
     7→## 1  |  High-Level System Context
     8→
     9→```mermaid
    10→flowchart LR
    11→    subgraph Creators & Analysts
    12→        A[Creative Professional] -- Annotate / Remix --> B(UI / Dashboards)
    13→    end
    14→
    15→    subgraph CanvasCraft ML Studio
    16→        direction LR
    17→        B -- REST / SignalR --> C[Controller Layer<br/> • MLOps Orchestrator]
    18→        C --> D[Model Layer<br/> • Feature Store<br/> • Experiment Tracking<br/> • Model Registry]
    19→        C --> E[Compute Layer<br/> • Training Workers<br/> • GPU Pool]
    20→        D --> F((DB))
    21→        E --> F
    22→        D <-- Event Bus --> B
    23→    end
    24→
    25→    F -. Audits & Metrics .-> G[(Observability Stack)]
    26→```
    27→
    28→* The **View layer** (`dashboards`, `3-D canvases`) exposes rich, gallery-style insights to creators.  
    29→* The **Controller layer** centralizes orchestration: it builds, trains, evaluates and deploys models through an **MLOps Pipeline Pattern**.  
    30→* The **Model layer** persists all versioned assets—datasets, features, metrics, checkpoints—while raising **Observer events** for drift.

    39→| Pipeline orchestration  | Pipeline P

I have completed the architectural analysis and written a comprehensive refactoring plan to `/logs/agent/solution.md`. 

Here's a summary of the key findings:

## Summary

The CanvasCraft ML Studio is a **C# .NET 8 modular monolith** with **event-driven monitoring** using the **Observer Pattern**. The analysis traced the full data flow:

1. **API → Prediction Events**: `ServingController` tracks predictions via `IExperimentTrackingService`
2. **Subject → Observers**: `ModelServingSubject` publishes events to `DataDriftObserver` and `PerformanceFadeObserver`
3. **Drift Detection → Retraining**: When drift is detected, `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` subscribes to `IModelMonitor` and orchestrates retraining

**Proposed Microservice Architecture:**
- **Communication**: Asynchronous via existing **RabbitMQ** infrastructure (justified by ADR-002)
- **Data Flow**: Main API publishes `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent` → MonitoringService consumes and detects drift → publishes `RetrainingRequiredEvent` → Pipeline module triggers retraining

**Key Files Requiring Modification:**
- `Startup.cs`: Remove monitoring observer DI registrations
- `ServingController.cs`: Publish events to message bus
- `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs`: Subscribe to events from RabbitMQ instead of in-process observable
- `docker-compose.yml`: Add new `monitoring-service` container definition

    "content": "# 001 \u2013 Adopt a Modular-Monolith Architecture  \nStatus: Accepted  \nDate: 2024-06-08  \nDeciders: Core Architecture Working Group (CAWG)  \nSupersedes: *n/a*  \nTags: [`architecture`](#), [`modular-monolith`](#), [`csharp`](#), [`mlops`](#)\n\n---\n\n## 1. Context  \n\nCanvasCraft ML Studio is an end-to-end **MVC-driven MLOps platform** that targets creative professionals iterating on generative media.  \nWhile the business road-map forecasts multiple deployment targets (desktop, on-prem, cloud, edge), the immediate product goals are:\n\n* Rapid iteration on **feature-engineering palettes** and **hyper-parameter color-wheels**.  \n* Tight coupling between **experiment-tracking**, **feature store**, and **model registry** to guarantee lineage.  \n* A **reactive model-monitoring** feedback loop that must not fall out of sync with training pipelines.  \n* A single deployable artifact that remains **operationally simple** yet **modular enough** to allow multiple teams (Data Science, UX, DevOps) to collaborate in parallel.\n\nThe team evaluated the following architectural styles:\n\n| Candidate | Pros | Cons |\n|-----------|------|------|\n| Pure Micro-services | Independent deployability; granular scaling | YAGNI for current size; high operational overhead; transaction boundaries complicate ACID model registry |\n| **Modular Monolith (Internal Hexagons)** | Clear module boundaries; performant in-process calls; single deployment unit | Requires discipline to avoid \u201cbig ball of mud\u201d; limited horizontal scaling |\n| Packaged Plugins (OSGi style) | Hot-swappable \u201cbrush\u201d plugins; strict contracts | Added complexity to load/unload modules; less tooling in .NET ecosystem |\n| Serverless Functions | Zero-management infra; pay-per-use for burst training jobs | Cold-start latency for interactive \u201cgallery\u201d UI; cross-function state management painful |\n\nGiven current **team size**, the **need for synchronous cross-module transactions** (e.g., dataset \u2194 feature store \u2194 model registry), and the **desire to postpone DevOps overhead** until usage patterns stabilize, we choose the **Modular Monolith**.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Decision  \n\nWe will build CanvasCraft ML Studio as a **C# 8/9, .NET 8** modular monolith with the following rules:\n\n1. **Single Deployment Unit**  \n   A single Docker container / process hosts all modules (Train, Serve, Monitor, UX, etc.).\n2. **Explicit Module Boundaries**  \n   Modules are organized under `/src/{BoundedContext}.{Module}` namespaces, compiled into **separate class libraries** referenced by a thin *Composition Root* (Web / gRPC Host).\n3. **Internal Hexagonal Architecture** per module  \n   Each module exposes its own:\n   * `Application` layer (Use-Cases, CQRS commands/queries)  \n   * `Domain` layer (Aggregates, Value Objects, Domain Events)  \n   * `Infrastructure` layer (EF Core, Redis, Kafka, TensorRT, etc.)\n4. **Public Contracts** *(C# interfaces + OpenAPI)*  \n   Modules interact only via their `*.Contracts` assemblies to prevent direct reference leaks.\n5. **Shared Kernel** kept minimal  \n   Only cross-cutting primitives (e.g., `Result<T>`, `IEvent`, `IDomainNotification`) live here.\n6. **Dependency Inversion through Internal DI Container**  \n   All external dependencies are injected via `IServiceCollection` extensions located in each module\u2019s `Infrastructure` layer.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Consequences  \n\n### Positive  \n\n* \ud83d\ude80 **Velocity** \u2013 Teams commit to their modules without touching others; compile-time boundaries give rapid feedback.  \n* \ud83d\udd2c **Observability** \u2013 Since calls are in-process, **OpenTelemetry** tracing is cheap; back-pressure can be simulated with Polly policies.  \n* \ud83d\uddc3\ufe0f **Transactional Integrity** \u2013 The feature store and model registry execute in the same ACID transaction when needed (e.g., using EF Core `IDbContextTransaction`).  \n* \ud83d\udee0\ufe0f **Gradual Extraction Path** \u2013 If a module\u2019s load pattern grows, we can extract it into a micro-service by lifting its contract and infrastructure *without* rewriting domain code.\n\n### Negative / Risks  \n\n* \ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f **Discipline Required** \u2013 Nothing (besides CI linting) prevents developers from taking a rogue reference into another module\u2019s `Infrastructure` assembly.  \n* \ud83d\udcc8 **Limited Horizontal Scaling** \u2013 The entire monolith scales as one unit. Mitigation: run multiple container replicas behind a load balancer.  \n* \ud83d\udcbc **Deployment Blast Radius** \u2013 A change in any module triggers a full redeploy. Our blue-green pipeline must be robust.\n\n---\n\n## 4. Implementation Sketch  \n\n### 4.1. Directory / Namespace Layout  \n\n```\nCanvasCraftMLStudio/\n\u2502\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 src/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 SharedKernel/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 CanvasCraft.SharedKernel.csproj\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 ExperimentTracking/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Contracts/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Domain/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Application/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 Infrastructure/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 FeatureEngineering/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 ...\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 ModelRegistry/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 ...\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 ServingGallery/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 ...\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 WebHost/\n\u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500 CanvasCraft.WebHost.csproj\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 docs/\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 architecture/\n        \u2514\u2500\u2500 adr/\n            \u2514\u2500\u2500 ...\n```\n\n### 4.2. Composition Root (simplified)\n\n```csharp\n// CanvasCraft.WebHost/Program.cs\nusing CanvasCraft.SharedKernel;\nusing CanvasCraft.ExperimentTracking.Infrastructure;\nusing CanvasCraft.FeatureEngineering.Infrastructure;\nusing CanvasCraft.ModelRegistry.Infrastructure;\nusing CanvasCraft.ServingGallery.Infrastructure;\n\nvar builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);\nbuilder.Services\n    .AddSharedKernel()\n    .AddExperimentTrackingModule(builder.Configuration)\n    .AddFeatureEngineeringModule(builder.Configuration)\n    .AddModelRegistryModule(builder.Configuration)\n    .AddServingGalleryModule(builder.Configuration);\n\nbuilder.Services.AddControllers().AddNewtonsoftJson();\n\nvar app = builder.Build();\napp.MapControllers();\napp.Run();\n```\n\n### 4.3. Enforcing Boundaries via Roslyn Analyzer\n\nA custom Roslyn analyzer (loaded in `Directory.Build.props`) blocks forbidden references:\n\n```csharp\n[DiagnosticAnalyzer(LanguageNames.CSharp)]\npublic sealed class NoInfrastructureLeakAnalyzer : DiagnosticAnalyzer\n{\n    private static readonly DiagnosticDescriptor Rule = new(\n        id: \"CCMS001\",\n        title: \"No cross-module Infrastructure references\",\n        messageFormat: \"Project '{0}' should not reference '{1}.Infrastructure'\",\n        category: \"Architecture\",\n        defaultSeverity: DiagnosticSeverity.Error,\n        isEnabledByDefault: true);\n\n    public override ImmutableArray<DiagnosticDescriptor> SupportedDiagnostics => ImmutableArray.Create(Rule);\n\n    public override void Initialize(AnalysisContext context) =>\n        context.RegisterCompilationStartAction(start =>\n        {\n            var infraProjects = start.Compilation.ReferencedAssemblyNames\n                .Where(a => a.Name.EndsWith(\".Infrastructure\", StringComparison.Ordinal))\n                .ToHashSet(StringComparer.Ordinal);\n\n            start.RegisterSymbolAction(symbolContext =>\n            {\n                var assembly = symbolContext.Symbol.ContainingAssembly?.Name;\n                if (assembly is null || !assembly.EndsWith(\".Infrastructure\"))\n                {\n                    foreach (var infra in infraProjects)\n                    {\n                        if (symbolContext.Compilation.AssemblyName == infra.ToString())\n                            continue;\n\n                        symbolContext.ReportDiagnostic(\n                            Diagnostic.Create(Rule, Location.None, assembly, infra));\n                    }\n                }\n            }, SymbolKind.NamedType);\n        });\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Alternatives Considered  \n\n1. **Full Micro-Services** with gRPC & Kafka  \n   *Rejected* \u2013 Over-engineering at current scale; slows feature velocity.  \n2. **Serverless-First** using Azure Functions & Durable Orchestration  \n   *Rejected* \u2013 Real-time \u201cgallery\u201d UI would suffer cold starts; local dev experience poor.  \n3. **Plugin-Oriented (MEF) Desktop App**  \n   *Rejected* \u2013 Conflicts with requirement for cloud-native CI/CD and containerization.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Validation Plan  \n\n* Implement two pilot modules (**ExperimentTracking** and **FeatureEngineering**) under this architecture.  \n* Run performance benchmark: ingest \u2192 transform \u2192 model fit; target < 250 ms overhead vs. baseline script.  \n* Conduct *\u201cdesign spike\u201d* to extract ExperimentTracking into a micro-service after initial release and measure required refactor effort (< 8 story points target).  \n* Audit module boundaries via the Roslyn analyzer in every PR.\n\n---\n\n## 7. References  \n\n* \u201cMonolith First\u201d \u2013 Martin Fowler, 2015  \n* \u201cA Modular Monolith Architecture in .NET\u201d \u2013 Khorikov, 2023  \n* OpenTelemetry .NET Instrumentation Guidelines, v1.7  \n* Domain-Driven Design Tackling Complexity in the Heart of Software \u2013 Evans, 2004  \n\n---\n\n*This document is living; amendments require a new ADR.*",

    "content": "```markdown\n<!--\nFile: CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/002-event-driven-monitoring.md\nThis Architecture Decision Record (ADR) captures why CanvasCraft ML Studio\nadopted an event-driven, reactive monitoring subsystem.\n-->\n\n# 002 \u2014 Event-Driven Monitoring\n\n* Status: **Accepted**\n* Date: 2024-06-11\n* Deciders: Core Platform Team  \n* Supersedes: *none*  \n* Tags: monitoring, observer-pattern, event-bus, mlops, csharp\n\n---\n\n## 1. Context  \n\nCanvasCraft ML Studio serves creative professionals who demand instant\nfeedback when a model\u2019s aesthetic *or* quantitative performance drifts.\nTraditional, pull-based dashboards proved too latent for interactive\nworkflows. We therefore require:\n\n* Near-real-time detection of data and model drift  \n* Reactive alerting to UI canvases, Slack, and WebHooks  \n* Loose coupling between producers (model training, feature store) and\n  consumers (dashboards, alerting services, auto-retrain jobs)  \n* A pluggable architecture that works in single-process testbeds **and**\n  distributed production clusters  \n\nThese constraints map naturally to an **Event-Driven Architecture (EDA)**\nimplemented via the **Observer Pattern**.\n\n---\n\n## 2. Decision  \n\nWe will implement a lightweight, in-process **Event Bus** backed by\n`System.Threading.Channels` for default deployments, with adapters that\nproxy to external brokers (Kafka / Azure Event Hubs) for scale-out\nenvironments. All monitoring signals will be published as immutable\ndomain events implementing `IModelEvent`. Down-stream subscribers may\nreact synchronously or asynchronously (e.g., stream to the dashboard,\nwrite to the Feature Store, or trigger auto-retraining).\n\n---\n\n## 3. Consequences  \n\n* + Producers/consumers remain oblivious of each other  \n* + Local unit tests stay fast by using the in-memory bus  \n* + Scaling to cloud brokers is a deployment concern, not a code change  \n* \u2212 Requires disciplined event-schema versioning  \n* \u2212 Potential complexity in distributed tracing (mitigated by\n  correlation IDs baked into `IModelEvent`)  \n\n---\n\n## 4. Reference Implementation (C#)\n\n```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Runtime.CompilerServices;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Channels;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.MLStudio.Monitoring\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Base contract for all domain events emitted by the ML Studio.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IModelEvent\n    {\n        DateTimeOffset OccurredOn { get; }\n        Guid CorrelationId { get; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Example event raised when feature or prediction drift is detected.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record DriftDetectedEvent(\n        string ModelName,\n        double DriftScore,\n        string DriftType,\n        DateTimeOffset OccurredOn,\n        Guid CorrelationId) : IModelEvent;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Thread-safe, in-memory event bus using <see cref=\"Channel{T}\"/> for high throughput.\n    /// An external adapter can bridge messages to Kafka, RabbitMQ, etc.\n    /// </summary>\n    public class InMemoryEventBus : IEventBus, IDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly Channel<IModelEvent> _channel;\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<Type, List<Func<IModelEvent, ValueTask>>> _subscriptions;\n        private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cts = new();\n        private readonly Task _dispatcherTask;\n\n        public InMemoryEventBus(int boundedCapacity = 10_000)\n        {\n            _channel = Channel.CreateBounded<IModelEvent>(new BoundedChannelOptions(boundedCapacity)\n            {\n                FullMode = BoundedChannelFullMode.Wait,\n                SingleReader = true,\n                SingleWriter = false\n            });\n            _subscriptions = new();\n            _dispatcherTask = Task.Run(DispatchLoopAsync, _cts.Token);\n        }\n\n        public async ValueTask PublishAsync(IModelEvent @event, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(@event);\n            ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n            await _channel.Writer.WriteAsync(@event, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n\n        public void Subscribe<TEvent>(Func<TEvent, ValueTask> handler) where TEvent : IModelEvent\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(handler);\n            var list = _subscriptions.GetOrAdd(typeof(TEvent), _ => new());\n            ValueTask Wrapper(IModelEvent e) => handler((TEvent)e);\n            list.Add(Wrapper);\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            _cts.Cancel();\n            _channel.Writer.Complete();\n            try { _dispatcherTask.Wait(TimeSpan.FromSeconds(5)); }\n            catch (AggregateException) { /* swallow */ }\n            _cts.Dispose();\n        }\n\n        // Core dispatcher: fan-out each event to its type-based subscribers.\n        private async Task DispatchLoopAsync()\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                while (await _channel.Reader.WaitToReadAsync(_cts.Token).ConfigureAwait(false))\n                {\n                    while (_channel.Reader.TryRead(out var evt))\n                    {\n                        if (_subscriptions.TryGetValue(evt.GetType(), out var handlers))\n                        {\n                            foreach (var h in handlers)\n                            {\n                                _ = SafeInvokeAsync(h, evt, _cts.Token);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n            catch (OperationCanceledException) { /* graceful shutdown */ }\n        }\n\n        [MethodImpl(MethodImplOptions.AggressiveInlining)]\n        private static async Task SafeInvokeAsync(\n            Func<IModelEvent, ValueTask> handler,\n            IModelEvent evt,\n            CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            try { await handler.Invoke(evt); }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                // TODO: emit a MonitoringExceptionEvent or log via ILogger\n                Console.Error.WriteLine($\"Handler failure: {ex}\");\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Abstraction to decouple components from the concrete bus implementation.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IEventBus\n    {\n        ValueTask PublishAsync(IModelEvent @event, CancellationToken ct = default);\n        void Subscribe<TEvent>(Func<TEvent, ValueTask> handler) where TEvent : IModelEvent;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Service that watches for drift events and triggers auto-retraining.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class AutoRetrainService\n    {\n        private readonly IEventBus _bus;\n\n        public AutoRetrainService(IEventBus bus)\n        {\n            _bus = bus;\n            _bus.Subscribe<DriftDetectedEvent>(OnDriftAsync);\n        }\n\n        private async ValueTask OnDriftAsync(DriftDetectedEvent evt)\n        {\n            Console.WriteLine(\n                $\"[AutoRetrain] {evt.ModelName} drifted ({evt.DriftType}:{evt.DriftScore:F2}). \" +\n                $\"CorrelationId={evt.CorrelationId}\");\n            // TODO: enqueue retraining pipeline job via orchestrator.\n            await Task.CompletedTask;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Example usage in composition root.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class MonitoringBootstrap\n    {\n        public static async Task DemonstrateAsync()\n        {\n            using var bus = new InMemoryEventBus();\n            var autoretrain = new AutoRetrainService(bus);\n\n            var driftEvent = new DriftDetectedEvent(\n                ModelName: \"StyleGAN-Canvas-v3\",\n                DriftScore: 0.42,\n                DriftType: \"KL Divergence\",\n                OccurredOn: DateTimeOffset.UtcNow,\n                CorrelationId: Guid.NewGuid());\n\n            await bus.PublishAsync(driftEvent);\n            await Task.Delay(500); // Give dispatcher time to deliver\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5. Roll-Out Plan  \n\n1. Merge reference implementation behind a feature flag  \n2. Instrument existing training jobs to publish `DriftDetectedEvent`,\n   `MetricThresholdBreachedEvent`, etc.  \n3. Incrementally migrate legacy polling dashboards to consume events  \n4. Enable Kafka adapter in production clusters for horizontal scale  \n\n---\n\n## 6. Alternatives Considered  \n\n* **Polling**: Rejected due to latency and tight coupling  \n* **Direct Service Calls**: Violates Open/Closed principle as new\n  consumers would require producer changes  \n* **Third-party APM only**: Complementary but does not provide\n  domain-specific semantics (e.g., aesthetic drift)  \n\n---\n\n## 7. References  \n\n* E. Gamma et al. *Design Patterns* \u2014 Observer  \n* M. Fowler \u2014 *Event Sourcing*  \n* Krizhevsky, *et al.* \u2014 *Imagenet Classification with Deep Convolutional\n  Neural Networks* (early drift discussion)\n```",

[ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status400BadRequest)]\n        [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status404NotFound)]\n        [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError)]\n        public async Task<IActionResult> PredictAsync(\n            [FromRoute] string modelName,\n            [FromBody] PredictionRequestDto request,\n            CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(modelName))\n            {\n                return BadRequest(\"Model name must be provided.\");\n            }\n\n            if (request?.Features is null || loop.\n                var predictionId = Guid.NewGuid().ToString(\"N\");\n                await _trackingService.TrackPredictionAsync(\n                    new PredictionEvent\n                    {\n                        Id = predictionId,\n                        ModelId = manifest.Id,\n                        ModelVersion = manifest.Version,\n                        TimestampUtc = [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status202Accepted)]\n        [ProducesResponseType(StatusCodes.Status404NotFound)]\n        public async Task<IActionResult> ReloadModelAsync(\n            [FromRoute] string modelName,\n            CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                var manifest = await _modelRegistry.GetLatestModelAsync(modelName, ct);\n                if (manifest is null) return NotFound();\n\n                await _inferenceService.ReloadModelAsync(manifest, ct);\n                return Accepted($\"Model '{modelName}' successfully reloaded.\");\n            }\n            catch (ModelRegistryException ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Model registry failure for model {ModelName}.\", modelName);\n                return NotFound(ex.Message);\n            }\n            catch (InferenceException ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to reload model {ModelName}.\",     "content": "```csharp\n// File: CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Observers/DataDriftObserver.cs\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.Events;\nusing CanvasCraft.FeatureStore;\nusing CanvasCraft.Monitoring.Alerts;\nusing CanvasCraft.Monitoring.Metrics;\nusing CanvasCraft.Shared;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.Monitoring.Observers\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Observes incoming <see cref=\"DataBatchEvent\"/> streams and computes data\u2013drift statistics\n    /// (currently PSI) against the baseline training distribution stored in the Feature Store.\n    /// When drift crosses the configured threshold, an alert is routed to the <see cref=\"IAlertService\"/>.\n    /// All metrics\u2014alerting or not\u2014are shipped to the configured <see cref=\"IMetricSink\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class DataDriftObserver : IObserver<DataBatchEvent>, IDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly IFeatureStatisticsRepository _baselineRepo;\n        private readonly IMetricSink _metricSink;\n        private readonly IAlertService _alertService;\n        private readonly DataDriftObserverOptions _options;\n        private readonly ILogger<DataDriftObserver> _logger;\n        private readonly IDisposable _subscription;\n        private readonly SemaphoreSlim _gate = new(1, 1);\n\n        // Cache baseline statistics for performance; keyed by feature name.\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, FeatureHistogram> _baselineCache = new();\n\n        public DataDriftObserver(\n            IObservable<DataBatchEvent> source,\n            IFeatureStatisticsRepository baselineRepo,\n            IMetricSink metricSink,\n            IAlertService alertService,\n            DataDriftObserverOptions options,\n            ILogger<DataDriftObserver> logger)\n        {\n            _baselineRepo = baselineRepo ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(baselineRepo));\n            _metricSink   = metricSink   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(metricSink));\n            _alertService = alertService ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(alertService));\n            _options      = options      ?? DataDriftObserverOptions.Default;\n            _logger       = logger       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n            _subscription = (source ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(source))).Subscribe(this);\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"DataDriftObserver initialized with AlertThreshold={Threshold:P2} BinCount={BinCount}.\",\n                _options.AlertThreshold, _options.BinCount);\n        }\n\n        #region IObserver<DataBatchEvent>\n\n        public async void OnNext(DataBatchEvent batch)\n        {\n            if (batch == null || batch.Records.Count == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Ignoring empty DataBatchEvent.\");\n                return;\n            }\n\n            try\n            {\n                await _gate.WaitAsync().ConfigureAwait(false);\n                ProcessBatch(batch);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Failed to process DataBatchEvent for ExperimentId={ExperimentId}.\",\n                    batch.ExperimentId);\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                _gate.Release();\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void OnError(Exception error)\n        {\n            _logger.LogError(error, \"Data source signaled an error to DataDriftObserver.\");\n        }\n\n        public void OnCompleted()\n        {\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Data source completed. DataDriftObserver shutting down.\");\n            Dispose();\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        private void ProcessBatch(DataBatchEvent batch)\n        {\n            foreach (var feature in batch.Signature.Features.Where(f => f.Type == FeatureType.Numeric))\n            {\n                var actualHistogram = BuildHistogram(batch.Records.Select(r => r.GetNumericValue(feature.Name)));\n\n                var baselineHistogram = _baselineCache.GetOrAdd(feature.Name, name =>\n                {\n                    // Fetch baseline from repository lazily\n                    var baselineStats = _baselineRepo.GetHistogram(batch.TrainingRunId, name);\n                    return baselineStats ?? throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                        $\"Baseline statistics for feature '{name}' not found.\");\n                });\n\n                var psi = ComputePsi(baselineHistogram, actualHistogram);\n\n                EmitMetrics(batch, feature.Name, psi);\n\n                if (psi >= _options.AlertThreshold)\n                {\n                    RaiseAlert(batch, feature.Name, psi);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        #region Alerting & Metrics\n\n        private void EmitMetrics(DataBatchEvent batch, string featureName, double psi)\n        {\n            var tags = new MetricTags(\n                (\"experiment_id\", batch.ExperimentId.ToString()),\n                (\"feature\", featureName));\n\n            _metricSink.RecordGauge(\"canvascraft.data_drift.psi\", psi, tags);\n        }\n\n        private void RaiseAlert(DataBatchEvent batch, string featureName, double psi)\n        {\n            var alert = new AlertMessage(\n                title: \"Data drift detected\",\n                body: $\"PSI={psi:F4} exceeded threshold for feature '{featureName}' in experiment {batch.ExperimentId}.\",\n                severity: AlertSeverity.Warning,\n                source: nameof(DataDriftObserver));\n\n            _alertService.Publish(alert);\n\n            _logger.LogWarning(\"Data drift detected (PSI={PSI:F4}) for feature '{Feature}' in ExperimentId={ExperimentId}.\",\n                psi, featureName, batch.ExperimentId);\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region Histogram & PSI\n\n        private FeatureHistogram BuildHistogram(IEnumerable<double> values)\n        {\n            var histogram = new FeatureHistogram(_options.BinCount);\n\n            foreach (var v in values.Where(x => !double.IsNaN(x) && !double.IsInfinity(x)))\n            {\n                histogram.Add(v);\n            }\n\n            histogram.Seal(); // finalize bin sizes & probabilities\n            return histogram;\n        }\n\n        private static double ComputePsi(FeatureHistogram expected, FeatureHistogram actual)\n        {\n            Guard.Against(expected.BinCount != actual.BinCount,\n                $\"Expected and actual histograms must have same bin count to compute PSI. \" +\n                $\"Expected={expected.BinCount}, Actual={actual.BinCount}\");\n\n            double psi = 0.0;\n            for (var i = 0; i < expected.BinCount; i++)\n            {\n                var expP = expected.BinProbabilities[i];\n                var actP = actual.BinProbabilities[i];\n\n                // Avoid division by zero / log(0)\n                if (expP <= 0 || actP <= 0)\n                {\n                    // Conventional approach: ignore bins with zero probability in either distribution\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                psi += (actP - expP) * Math.Log(actP / expP);\n            }\n            return psi;\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region IDisposable\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            _subscription?.Dispose();\n            _gate?.Dispose();\n            GC.SuppressFinalize(this);\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Configuration options for <see cref=\"DataDriftObserver\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record DataDriftObserverOptions\n    {\n        public double AlertThreshold { get; init; } = 0.25;     // typical PSI threshold\n        public int    BinCount       { get; init; } = 10;       // default number of histogram bins\n\n        public static DataDriftObserverOptions Default => new();\n    }\n\n    #region Helper Types\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Lightweight histogram that tracks bin boundaries and probabilities for PSI calculation.\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class FeatureHistogram\n    {\n        private readonly List<double> _values = new();\n        private readonly int _binCount;\n        private bool _sealed;\n        private double _min;\n        private double _max;\n\n        public int BinCount => _binCount;\n        public IReadOnlyList<double> BinProbabilities => _probabilities;\n\n        private readonly double[] _probabilities;\n\n        public FeatureHistogram(int binCount)\n        {\n            if (binCount <= 0) throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(binCount));\n\n            _binCount = binCount;\n            _probabilities = new double[_binCount];\n        }\n\n        public void Add(double value)\n        {\n            if (_sealed) throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Cannot add value after histogram is sealed.\");\n\n            if (_values.Count == 0)\n            {\n                _min = _max = value;\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                if (value < _min) _min = value;\n                if (value > _max) _max = value;\n            }\n            _values.Add(value);\n        }\n\n        public void Seal()\n        {\n            if (_sealed) return;\n\n            var binWidth = (_max - _min) / _binCount;\n\n            // Handle edge case: constant feature\n            if (binWidth.Equals(0.0))\n            {\n                _probabilities[0] = 1.0;\n                _sealed = true;\n                return;\n            }\n\n            foreach (var v in _values)\n            {\n                var index = (int)((v - _min) / binWidth);\n                if (index == _binCount) index--; // Right\u2013inclusive correction\n                _probabilities[index]++;\n            }\n\n            var total = _values.Count;\n            for (var i = 0; i < _probabilities.Length; i++)\n            {\n                _probabilities[i] /= total;\n            }\n\n            _sealed = true;\n            _values.Clear();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

       private void PublishInternal(ServingEventBase evt)\n        {\n            if (_disposed) return;\n\n            var tasks = new List<Task>(_observers.Count);\n\n            foreach (var        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            if (_disposed) return;\n\n            _disposed = true;\n            _cancellationTokenSource.Cancel();\n\n            // Inform observers that the     "content": "```csharp\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Concurrent;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.Logging;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.ModelMonitoring;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.ModelRegistry;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.Orchestration;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.Tracing;\nusing CanvasCraft.Core.Utils;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.Pipeline.Triggers\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Subscribes to <see cref=\"IModelMonitor\" /> events (e.g. data / concept drift, performance decay) and\n    ///     automatically kicks off a retraining pipeline when thresholds are violated.\n    ///\n    ///     The class implements <see cref=\"IObserver{T}\" /> so that it can be chained into the wider\n    ///     Observer/Reactive-streams that power the CanvasCraft runtime.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class AutomatedRetrainingTrigger : IObserver<ModelDriftReport>, IDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cts             = new();\n        private readonly IEventLogger            _logger;\n        private readonly IModelTrainingOrchestrator _orchestrator;\n        private readonly IExperimentTracker      _tracker;\n        private readonly IModelRegistry          _registry;\n\n        // Debounce protection \u2013 avoid flooding if several monitors publish concurrently.\n        private readonly TimeSpan _debounceWindow;\n        private readonly ConcurrentQueue<ModelDriftReport> _inboundQueue = new();\n        private readonly PeriodicTimer _pollTimer;\n\n        // Async-exclusive to guarantee single active retraining job.\n        private readonly AsyncLock _retrainLock = new();\n\n        private bool _disposed;\n\n        public AutomatedRetrainingTrigger(\n            IModelMonitor                monitor,\n            IModelTrainingOrchestrator   orchestrator,\n            IExperimentTracker           tracker,\n            IModelRegistry               registry,\n            IEventLogger                 logger,\n            TimeSpan?                    debounceWindow = null,\n            TimeSpan?                    pollInterval   = null)\n        {\n            _orchestrator   = orchestrator  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(orchestrator));\n            _tracker        = tracker       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(tracker));\n            _registry       = registry      ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(registry));\n            _logger         = logger        ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            _debounceWindow = debounceWindow ?? TimeSpan.FromSeconds(30);\n            _pollTimer      = new PeriodicTimer(pollInterval ?? TimeSpan.FromSeconds(5));\n\n            // Subscribe to the monitor stream.\n            monitor.Subscribe(this);\n            _ = Task.Run(ProcessInboundQueueAsync, _cts.Token);\n        }\n\n        #region Observer implementation\n\n        public void OnNext(ModelDriftReport value)\n        {\n            _inboundQueue.Enqueue(value);\n        }\n\n        public void OnCompleted()\n        {\n            _logger.Info(\"[RetrainingTrigger] Monitor stream completed.\");\n        }\n\n        public void OnError(Exception error)\n        {\n            _logger.Error(error, \"[RetrainingTrigger] Monitor stream faulted.\");\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region Queue Processing\n\n        private async Task ProcessInboundQueueAsync()\n        {\n            var driftBuffer = new List<ModelDriftReport>();\n\n            try\n            {\n                while (await _pollTimer.WaitForNextTickAsync(_cts.Token))\n                {\n                    driftBuffer.Clear();\n\n                    // Drain queue fast.\n                    while (_inboundQueue.TryDequeue(out var report))\n                    {\n                        driftBuffer.Add(report);\n                    }\n\n                    if (driftBuffer.Count == 0)\n                        continue;\n\n                    // Collapse into a single aggregate report.\n                    var aggregate = ModelDriftReport.Aggregate(driftBuffer);\n                    if (!aggregate.ShouldRetrain)\n                    {\n                        _logger.Debug(\"[RetrainingTrigger] Drift detected but below thresholds. Ignoring.\");\n                        continue;\n                    }\n\n                    // Guard against rapid-fire triggers using a timestamped throttle.\n                    var lastRetrainTime = await _tracker.GetLastRetrainTimestampAsync(aggregate.ModelId, _cts.Token);\n                    if (lastRetrainTime.HasValue &&\n                        DateTimeOffset.UtcNow - lastRetrainTime.Value < _debounceWindow)\n                    {\n                        _logger.Info(\n                            \"[RetrainingTrigger] Retrain already triggered recently for model {ModelId}. Skipping.\",\n                            aggregate.ModelId);\n                        continue;\n                    }\n\n                    await TriggerRetrainingAsync(aggregate);\n                }\n            }\n            catch (OperationCanceledException)\n            {\n                // Normal shutdown.\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.Error(ex, \"[RetrainingTrigger] Unhandled error in queue processor.\");\n            }\n        }\n\n        private async Task TriggerRetrainingAsync(ModelDriftReport report)\n        {\n            using var retrainGuard = await _retrainLock.TryAcquireAsync(_cts.Token);\n            if (!retrainGuard.Acquired)\n            {\n                _logger.Info(\"[RetrainingTrigger] Retrain already in progress. Skipping new trigger.\");\n                return;\n            }\n\n            var retrainCtx = BuildContext(report);\n\n            try\n            {\n                _logger.Info(\n                    \"[RetrainingTrigger] Starting automated retraining for model {ModelId}, drift={DriftScore:P2}\",\n                    report.ModelId,\n                    report.DriftScore);\n\n                var experimentId = await _tracker.StartExperimentAsync(retrainCtx, _cts.Token);\n\n                var result = await _orchestrator.RetrainAsync(retrainCtx, _cts.Token);\n\n                await _tracker.CompleteExperimentAsync(experimentId, result, _cts.Token);\n                await _registry.RegisterNewModelAsync(result.ModelArtifact, _cts.Token);\n\n                _logger.Info(\n                    \"[RetrainingTrigger] Completed retraining for model {ModelId}. New version: {Version}\",\n                    report.ModelId,\n                    result.ModelArtifact.Version);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.Error(ex,\n                    \"[RetrainingTrigger] Automated retraining failed for model {ModelId}\",\n                    report.ModelId);\n\n                await _tracker.FailExperimentAsync(retrainCtx.ExperimentId, ex, CancellationToken.None);\n            }\n        }\n\n        private RetrainingContext BuildContext(ModelDriftReport report)\n        {\n            return new RetrainingContext(\n                report.ModelId,\n                report.DatasetId,\n                report.DriftScore,\n                triggerType: RetrainingTriggerType.Automated,\n                triggeredAt: DateTimeOffset.UtcNow);\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region IDisposable\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            if (_disposed) return;\n            _disposed = true;\n\n            _cts.Cancel();\n            _pollTimer.Dispose();\n            _cts.Dispose();\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    #region Supporting types (would normally live in separate source files)\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Represents a model drift or decay report emitted by <see cref=\"IModelMonitor\" />.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record ModelDriftReport(\n        string ModelId,\n        string DatasetId,\n        double DriftScore,\n        DateTimeOffset ObservedAt,\n        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, double> Metrics)\n    {\n        public bool ShouldRetrain => DriftScore >= 0.1; // Example threshold.\n\n        public static ModelDriftReport Aggregate(IEnumerable<ModelDriftReport> reports)\n        {\n            var list = reports.ToList();\n\n            return new ModelDriftReport(\n                list.First().ModelId,\n                list.First().DatasetId,\n                list.Max(r => r.DriftScore),\n                list.Max(r => r.ObservedAt),\n                list.SelectMany(r => r.Metrics).GroupBy(kv => kv.Key)\n                    .ToDictionary(g => g.Key, g => g.Average(kv => kv.Value)));\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Represents the context required for retraining.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record RetrainingContext(\n        string           ModelId,\n        string           DatasetId,\n        double           DriftScore,\n        RetrainingTriggerType TriggerType,\n        DateTimeOffset   TriggeredAt,\n        Guid?            ExperimentId = null);\n\n    public enum RetrainingTriggerType\n    {\n        Automated,\n        Manual,\n        Scheduled\n    }\n\n    public interface IModelMonitor : IObservable<ModelDriftReport> { }\n\n    public interface IModelTrainingOrchestrator\n    {\n        Task<ModelTrainingResult> RetrainAsync(RetrainingContext context, CancellationToken token);\n    }\n\n    public interface IExperimentTracker\n    {\n        Task<Guid> StartExperimentAsync(RetrainingContext context, CancellationToken token);\n        Task CompleteExperimentAsync(Guid experimentId, ModelTrainingResult result, CancellationToken token);\n        Task FailExperimentAsync(Guid experimentId, Exception error, CancellationToken token);\n        Task<DateTimeOffset?> GetLastRetrainTimestampAsync(string modelId, CancellationToken token);\n    }\n\n    public interface IModelRegistry\n    {\n        Task RegisterNewModelAsync(ModelArtifact artifact, CancellationToken token);\n    }\n\n    public sealed record ModelTrainingResult(ModelArtifact ModelArtifact, IDictionary<string, double> Metrics);\n\n    public sealed record ModelArtifact(string ModelId, string Version, Uri StorageUri);\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

  /// </summary>\n        public void Configure(IApplicationBuilder app, ILogger<Startup> logger)\n        {\n            // Global exception handler (must be first)\n _environment.EnvironmentName);\n        }\n\n        #region Helper methods / nested types\n\n        private static Task WriteHealthResponse(HttpContext context, HealthReport report)\n        {\n            context.Response.ContentType = \"application/json\";\n            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(new\n            {\n                status   = report.Status.ToString(),\n                details  = report.Entries.Select(e => new\n                {\n                    name   = e.Key,\n                    state  = e.Value.Status.ToString(),\n                    error  = ErrorHandlingMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, ILogger<ErrorHandlingMiddleware> logger)\n            {\n                _next   = next;\n                _logger = logger;\n            }\n\n            public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext context)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    await _next(context);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Unhandled exception caught by global middleware.\");\n\n                    var problem = new ProblemDetails\n                    {\n                        Status = StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError,\n                        Title  = \"An internal server error occurred.\",\n                        Detail = _environment?.IsDevelopment() == true ? ex.ToString() : \"Please contact support.\"\n                    };\n\n                    context.Response.ContentType = \"application/problem+json\";\n                    context.Response.StatusCode  = problem.Status ?? StatusCodes.Status500InternalServerError;\n                    await context.Response.WriteAsJsonAsync(problem);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n}\n```\n",

ILogger<RabbitMqService> logger,\n            IHostApplicationLifetime lifetime)\n        {\n            _options = options?.Value ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(options));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n            _connectionRetryPolicy = Policy\n                .Handle<BrokerUnreachableException>()\n                .Or<SocketException>()\n                .WaitAndRetryForever(\n                    retryAttempt => TimeSpan.FromSeconds(Math.Min(retryAttempt, 30)),\n                    (ex, ts) =>\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"RabbitMQ connection attempt failed, retrying in {Delay}s\", ts.TotalSeconds);\n                    });\n\n            _publishRetryPolicy =                {\n                    channel.BasicNack(ea.DeliveryTag, multiple: false, requeue: true);\n                    return;\n                }\n\n                try\n                {\n Nack with requeue=false\");\n                    channel.BasicNack(deliveryTag: ea.DeliveryTag, multiple: false, requeue: false);\n                }\n            };\n\n            string consumerTag = channel.BasicConsume(\n                queue: queue,\n                autoAck: false,\n                consumer: consumer);\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Subscribed to queue '{Queue}' with consumer tag '{ConsumerTag}'\", queue, consumerTag);\n\n            IDisposable subscription = new Subscription(channel, consumerTag, _logger);\n\n            // Allow awaiting to satisfy async signature\n            await Task.CompletedTask;\n\n            return subscription;\n        }\n\n        private static TMessage?            {\n                    Uri = new Uri(_options.ConnectionUri),\n                    DispatchConsumersAsync = true,\n                    RequestedConnectionTimeout = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(10)\n                };\n\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Attempting to connect to RabbitMQ at {Uri}\", _options.ConnectionUri);\n                var connection = factory.CreateConnection();\n                connection.ConnectionShutdown += OnConnectionShutdown;\n                return connection;\n            });\n        }\n\n        private IModel Dispose();\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            if (_disposed) return;\n            _disposed = true;\n\n            foreach (var channel in _channels.Values)\n            {\n                if (channel.IsOpen)\n                    channel.Close();\n                channel.Dispose();\n            }\n\n            _channels.Clear();\n\n            if (_connection.IsOpen)\n                _connection.Close();\n\n            _connection.Dispose();\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"RabbitMQ service disposed.\");\n        }\n\n        private void disposed.\", _consumerTag);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Error disposing consumer '{ConsumerTag}'\", _consumerTag);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n}\n```",

A thin abstraction layer designed to keep domain\n//              services decoupled from the concrete transport (e.g. RabbitMQ, Azure Service Bus,\n//              in-memory testing harness).\n// -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.Core.Interfaces.Services\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Marker interface for all messages that travel through <see cref=\"IMessageBus\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IMessage\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Globally unique identifier for the message instance.\n        /// </summary>\n        Guid Id { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// UTC timestamp indicating when the message was created.\n        /// </summary>\n        DateTimeOffset TimestampUtc { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Optional bag of key/value pairs for meta-data or tracing headers.\n        /// </summary>\n        IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> Headers { get; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Represents a one-way notification that expresses something that already happened.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDomainEvent : IMessage { }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Represents an instruction to perform a task. Should be handled exactly once.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface ICommand : IMessage { }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Represents a request that expects a response of type <typeparamref name=\"TResponse\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <typeparam name=\"TResponse\">The type of the expected response.</typeparam>\n    public interface IRequest<TResponse> : IMessage { }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Options that influence how a subscription behaves.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class SubscriptionOptions\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Maximum number of concurrent message handlers allowed. Default is <see cref=\"Environment.ProcessorCount\"/>.\n        /// </summary>\n        public int MaxDegreeOfParallelism { get; init; } = Environment.ProcessorCount;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Defines the Quality-of-Service level desired for this subscription.\n        /// </summary>\n        public QoS QualityOfService { get; init; } = QoS.AtLeastOnce;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Indicates whether the subscription should automatically retry failed messages.\n        /// </summary>\n        public bool EnableRetry { get; init; } = true;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// If <see cref=\"EnableRetry\"/> is true, defines the maximum number of retry attempts.\n        /// </summary>\n        public int MaxRetryAttempts { get; init; } = 5;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Quality of Service guarantees offered by the bus implementation.\n    /// </summary>\n    public enum QoS\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Message may be delivered zero or more times.\n        /// </summary>\n        AtMostOnce,\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Message will be delivered at least once. Handlers must be idempotent.\n        /// </summary>\n        AtLeastOnce,\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Message will be delivered exactly once. Requires support from underlying broker.\n        /// </summary>\n        ExactlyOnce\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// The core abstraction that enables publish/subscribe, command dispatching and request/response\n    /// semantics for the entire CanvasCraft platform.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IMessageBus\n    {\n        #region Publish / Send\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Publishes a domain event to all registered subscribers. options = null,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n            where TCommand : ICommand;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Registers a request handler that can reply with <typeparamref name=\"TResponse\"/>.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"TRequest\">The request type.</typeparam>\n        /// <typeparam name=\"TResponse\">The response type.</typeparam>\n        /// <param name=\"handler\">Delegate that processes the request and returns a response.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"options\">Subscription tuning options.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Token to cancel the subscription.</param>\n        IDisposable RegisterRequestHandler<TRequest, TResponse>(\n            Func<TRequest, CancellationToken, Task<TResponse>> handler,\n            SubscriptionOptions? Audits & Metrics .-> G[(Observability Stack)]\n```\n\n* The **View layer** (`dashboards`, `3-D canvases`) exposes rich, gallery-style insights to creators.  \n* The **Controller layer** centralizes orchestration: it builds, trains, evaluates and deploys models through an **MLOps Pipeline Pattern**.  \n* The **Model layer** persists all versioned assets\u2014datasets, features, metrics, comments** and follow **.NET 8** conventions (nullable enabled, `ILogger<T>` injection, async/await).\n\n---\n\n## 3  |  Representative Code Snippets\n\n> The following excerpts are lifted directly Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.ML.Factories;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Produces concrete <see cref=\"IPreprocessingBrush\"/> instances at runtime, enabling\n/// creators to dynamically \"swap brushes\" without recompilation.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class BrushFactory\n{\n    private readonly ILogger<BrushFactory> _logger;\n\n    public BrushFactory(ILogger<BrushFactory> logger)\n        => _logger = logger;\n\n    public IPreprocessingBrush Create(BrushType type) => type switch\n    {\n        BrushType.StandardScaler      => new StandardScalerBrush(),\n        BrushType.ImageAugmenter       => new ImageAugmenterBrush(),\n        BrushType.AudioSpectrogrammer  => new AudioSpectrogramBrush(),\n        _ => throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(type), type, \"Unsupported brush type.\")\n    };\n}\n```\n\n### 3.2  MLOps Training Pipeline (Pipeline Pattern)\n\n```csharp\nnamespace CanvasCraft.ML.Pipeline;\n\npublic sealed class TrainingPipeline\n{\n    private readonly IList<IPipelineStep> _steps;\n\n    public TrainingPipeline(IEnumerable<IPipelineStep> steps)\n        => _steps = steps.ToList();\n\n    public async Task<PipelineContext> RunAsync(PipelineContext ctx, CancellationToken token = default)\n    {\n        foreach (var step in _steps)\n        {\n            ctx = await step.ExecuteAsync(ctx, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            if (ctx.Status is PipelineStatus.Failed)\n                break;\n        }\n\n        return ctx;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### 3.3  Model Drift Observer\n\n```csharp\nusing CanvasCraft.ML.Events;\nusing MediatR;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.ML.Observer;\n\npublic sealed class ModelDriftDetector : INotificationHandler<DriftEvent>\n{\n    private readonly ILogger<ModelDriftDetector> _logger;\n\n    public ModelDriftDetector(ILogger<ModelDriftDetector> logger)\n        => _logger = logger;\n\n    public Task Handle(DriftEvent notification, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        _logger.LogWarning(\n            \"\u26a0\ufe0f  Drift detected for ModelId={ModelId} (\u0394={Delta:P2}). Triggering retrain \u2026\",\n            notification.ModelId,\n            notification.Delta);\n\n        // Fire-and-forget; handled by retryable background job.\n        _ = notification.RetrainingCallback?.Invoke();\n\n        return Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4  |  Sequence Diagram \u2014 End-to-End Training Cycle\n\n```mermaid\nsequenceDiagram\n    participant UI\n    participant Controller\n    participant Pipeline\n    participant Worker\n    participant Registry\n\n    UI->>Controller: StartTraining(cmd)\n    Controller->>Pipeline: Build(ctx)\n    Pipeline->>Worker: Execute steps\n    Worker-->>Registry: Log metrics / checkpoint\n    Registry-->>UI: Stream artifacts\n    Worker-->>Controller: Completed(ctx)\n    Controller-->>UI: Publish results\n```\n\n---\n\n## 5  |  Error Handling & Observability\n\n1. Each **pipeline step** returns a `PipelineContext` holding `Status`, `Error`, and semantic metadata.  \n2. Unhandled exceptions bubble to the **global `ExceptionHandlerMiddleware`**, emitting structured logs to **OPENTELEMETRY** and `Grafana`.  \n3. All event notifications implement **`INotification` (MediatR)** allowing decoupled retries and circuit-breakers.\n\n---\n\n## 6  |  Roadmap Highlights\n\n- Port **training workers** to .NET 8 + CUDA for AOT speed-ups.  \n- Add a **DiffusionBrush** to support multimodal latent-space remixing.  \n- Extend the **Model Gallery** with in-browser WebGL inferencing.\n\n---\n\n> \u00a9 2024 CanvasCraft.  \n> Art meets Machine Learning \u2014 every model, a masterpiece.\n```",
