    "content": "```csharp\n// ===========================================\n// CanvasCraft ML Studio \u2013 Training Pipeline\n// File: TrainingPipeline.cs\n// Project: CanvasCraft ML Studio (ml_training)\n// ===========================================\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\nusing Microsoft.ML;\nusing Microsoft.ML.Data;\n\nnamespace CanvasCraft.MLStudio.Pipeline\n{\n    #region Pipeline Core\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Abstraction for a single step in the ML pipeline. Each step is observable and\n    /// can modify the shared <see cref=\"PipelineContext\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IPipelineStep\n    {\n        string Name { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes the step asynchronously.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token = default);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Raised whenever <see cref=\"Status\"/> changes.\n        /// </summary>\n        event EventHandler<PipelineStepStatusChangedEventArgs>? StatusChanged;\n\n        StepStatus Status { get; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Shared, mutable pipeline state. Acts as the glue that passes artifacts from step to step.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class PipelineContext\n    {\n        public IDataView? RawData { get; init; }\n        public IDataView? Features { get; set; }\n        public ITransformer? TrainedModel { get; set; }\n        public DataViewSchema? ModelSchema { get; set; }\n        public Dictionary<string, object> Properties { get; } = new(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase);\n\n        public T Get<T>(string key) => (T)Properties[key];\n        public void Set<T>(string key, T value) => Properties[key] = value;\n\n        public PipelineContext WithRawData(IDataView data) => this with { RawData = data };\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Concrete implementation of <see cref=\"IPipelineStep\"/> providing default error handling\n    /// and progress notifications.\n    /// </summary>\n    public abstract class PipelineStepBase : IPipelineStep\n    {\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n        private StepStatus _status = StepStatus.Pending;\n\n        protected PipelineStepBase(ILogger logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n        public abstract string Name { get; }\n\n        public StepStatus Status\n        {\n            get => _status;\n            protected set\n            {\n                if (_status == value) return;\n                _status = value;\n                StatusChanged?.Invoke(this, new PipelineStepStatusChangedEventArgs(Name, value, DateTimeOffset.UtcNow));\n            }\n        }\n\n        public event EventHandler<PipelineStepStatusChangedEventArgs>? StatusChanged;\n\n        public async Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                Status = StepStatus.Running;\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Step '{Step}' started.\", Name);\n\n                var result = await ExecuteCoreAsync(context, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                Status = StepStatus.Succeeded;\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Step '{Step}' succeeded.\", Name);\n                return result;\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                Status = StepStatus.Failed;\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Step '{Step}' failed.\", Name);\n                throw; // bubble up; pipeline orchestrator decides fate\n            }\n        }\n\n        protected abstract Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteCoreAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token);\n    }\n\n    public enum StepStatus\n    {\n        Pending,\n        Running,\n        Succeeded,\n        Failed,\n        Skipped\n    }\n\n    public sealed record PipelineStepStatusChangedEventArgs(string StepName, StepStatus Status, DateTimeOffset Timestamp);\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Concrete Steps\n\n    public sealed class DataIngestionStep : PipelineStepBase\n    {\n        private readonly Func<MLContext, IDataView> _dataLoader;\n        private readonly MLContext _mlContext;\n\n        public DataIngestionStep(MLContext mlContext, Func<MLContext, IDataView> dataLoader, ILogger<DataIngestionStep> logger)\n            : base(logger)\n        {\n            _mlContext = mlContext;\n            _dataLoader = dataLoader;\n        }\n\n        public override string Name => \"Data Ingestion\";\n\n        protected override Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteCoreAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            IDataView data = _dataLoader(_mlContext);\n            context = context.WithRawData(data);\n            return Task.FromResult(context);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public sealed class FeatureEngineeringStep : PipelineStepBase\n    {\n        private readonly IFeatureEngineeringStrategy _strategy;\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n        private readonly MLContext _mlContext;\n\n        public FeatureEngineeringStep(MLContext mlContext,\n                                      IFeatureEngineeringStrategy strategy,\n                                      ILogger<FeatureEngineeringStep> logger)\n            : base(logger)\n        {\n            _mlContext = mlContext;\n            _strategy = strategy;\n            _logger = logger;\n        }\n\n        public override string Name => \"Feature Engineering\";\n\n        protected override Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteCoreAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            if (context.RawData is null)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Raw data is required before feature engineering.\");\n\n            IDataView engineered = _strategy.Apply(_mlContext, context.RawData);\n            context.Features = engineered;\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Feature engineering produced schema: {Schema}\", engineered.Schema);\n            return Task.FromResult(context);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public sealed class ModelTrainingStep : PipelineStepBase\n    {\n        private readonly Func<MLContext, IEstimator<ITransformer>> _trainerFactory;\n        private readonly MLContext _mlContext;\n\n        public ModelTrainingStep(MLContext mlContext,\n                                 Func<MLContext, IEstimator<ITransformer>> trainerFactory,\n                                 ILogger<ModelTrainingStep> logger)\n            : base(logger)\n        {\n            _mlContext = mlContext;\n            _trainerFactory = trainerFactory;\n        }\n\n        public override string Name => \"Model Training\";\n\n        protected override async Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteCoreAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            if (context.Features is null)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Features are required before training.\");\n\n            IEstimator<ITransformer> pipeline = _trainerFactory(_mlContext);\n            var model = pipeline.Fit(context.Features);\n\n            context.TrainedModel = model;\n            context.ModelSchema = context.Features.Schema;\n\n            // Simulate async training for long-running tasks\n            await Task.Yield();\n            return context;\n        }\n    }\n\n    public sealed class ModelEvaluationStep : PipelineStepBase\n    {\n        private readonly Func<MLContext, IDataView> _testDataLoader;\n        private readonly MLContext _mlContext;\n\n        public ModelEvaluationStep(MLContext mlContext,\n                                   Func<MLContext, IDataView> testDataLoader,\n                                   ILogger<ModelEvaluationStep> logger)\n            : base(logger)\n        {\n            _mlContext = mlContext;\n            _testDataLoader = testDataLoader;\n        }\n\n        public override string Name => \"Model Evaluation\";\n\n        protected override Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteCoreAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            if (context.TrainedModel is null)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"A trained model is required for evaluation.\");\n\n            IDataView testData = _testDataLoader(_mlContext);\n\n            var predictions = context.TrainedModel.Transform(testData);\n            var metrics = _mlContext.BinaryClassification.Evaluate(predictions);\n\n            context.Set(\"metrics\", metrics);\n            return Task.FromResult(context);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public sealed class ModelRegistrationStep : PipelineStepBase\n    {\n        private readonly IModelRegistry _registry;\n\n        public ModelRegistrationStep(IModelRegistry registry, ILogger<ModelRegistrationStep> logger)\n            : base(logger) => _registry = registry;\n\n        public override string Name => \"Model Registration\";\n\n        protected override async Task<PipelineContext> ExecuteCoreAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token)\n        {\n            if (context.TrainedModel is null)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"A trained model must exist before registration.\");\n\n            var id = await _registry.RegisterAsync(context.TrainedModel, context.ModelSchema!, context.Properties, token)\n                                    .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            context.Set(\"modelId\", id);\n            return context;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Strategy + Factory\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Contract for feature engineering strategies.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IFeatureEngineeringStrategy\n    {\n        IDataView Apply(MLContext mlContext, IDataView input);\n    }\n\n    public sealed class DefaultFeatureEngineeringStrategy : IFeatureEngineeringStrategy\n    {\n        public IDataView Apply(MLContext mlContext, IDataView input)\n        {\n            var pipeline = mlContext.Transforms\n                                    .ReplaceMissingValues(\"Features\")\n                                    .NormalizeMinMax(\"Features\");\n            return pipeline.Fit(input).Transform(input);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Factory for obtaining a strategy based on runtime hints.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class FeatureEngineeringStrategyFactory\n    {\n        public static IFeatureEngineeringStrategy Create(string paletteName) =>\n            paletteName switch\n            {\n                \"default\" or null => new DefaultFeatureEngineeringStrategy(),\n                _ => throw new NotSupportedException($\"Palette '{paletteName}' is not supported.\")\n            };\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Observer\n\n    public interface IPipelineObserver\n    {\n        void OnStepStatusChanged(object? sender, PipelineStepStatusChangedEventArgs args);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Simple observer that writes step events to the supplied <see cref=\"ILogger\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class LoggingPipelineObserver : IPipelineObserver\n    {\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n\n        public LoggingPipelineObserver(ILogger<LoggingPipelineObserver> logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n        public void OnStepStatusChanged(object? sender, PipelineStepStatusChangedEventArgs args)\n        {\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"[{Time:o}] Step '{Step}' is {Status}\",\n                                   args.Timestamp, args.StepName, args.Status);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Orchestrator\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Orchestrates a series of <see cref=\"IPipelineStep\"/> instances, applying the Pipeline Pattern.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class TrainingPipeline\n    {\n        private readonly IList<IPipelineStep> _steps;\n        private readonly IList<IPipelineObserver> _observers;\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n\n        public TrainingPipeline(IList<IPipelineStep> steps,\n                                IEnumerable<IPipelineObserver>? observers,\n                                ILogger<TrainingPipeline> logger)\n        {\n            _steps      = steps ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(steps));\n            _observers  = observers is null ? new List<IPipelineObserver>() : new List<IPipelineObserver>(observers);\n            _logger     = logger;\n            WireUpObservers();\n        }\n\n        public async Task<PipelineContext> RunAsync(PipelineContext context, CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            foreach (var step in _steps)\n            {\n                token.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n                context = await step.ExecuteAsync(context, token).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Pipeline execution completed.\");\n            return context;\n        }\n\n        private void WireUpObservers()\n        {\n            foreach (var step in _steps)\n            {\n                step.StatusChanged += (_, args) =>\n                {\n                    foreach (var observer in _observers)\n                        observer.OnStepStatusChanged(step, args);\n                };\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region metadata,\n                                        CancellationToken token = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// In-memory registry for demo/testing purposes.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class InMemoryModelRegistry : IModelRegistry\n    {\n        private readonly Dictionary<string, (ITransformer model, DataViewSchema schema, DateTimeOffset timestamp)> _store = new();\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n\n        public InMemoryModelRegistry(ILogger<InMemoryModelRegistry> logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n        public ValueTask<string> RegisterAsync(ITransformer model, DataViewSchema schema,\n                                               IReadOnlyDictionary<string, object> metadata,\n                                               CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            string id = Guid.NewGuid().ToString(\"N\");\n            _store[id] = (model, schema, DateTimeOffset.UtcNow);\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Model registered with ID: {ModelId}\", id);\n            return ValueTask.FromResult(id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

Modular Monolith Architecture Decision (ADR-001)\n\n```markdown\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/001-modular-monolith-architecture.md\n// Lines: 29-52\n\nGiven current **team size**, the **need for synchronous cross-module transactions** (e.g., dataset \u2194 feature store \u2194 model registry), and the **desire to postpone DevOps overhead** until usage patterns stabilize, we choose the **Modular Monolith**.\n\n## 2. Decision\n\nWe will build CanvasCraft ML Studio as a **C# 8/9, .NET 8** modular monolith with the following rules:\n\n1. **Single Deployment Unit**\n   A single Docker container / process hosts all modules (Train, Serve, Monitor, UX, etc.).\n2. **Explicit Module Boundaries**\n   Modules are organized under `/src/{BoundedContext}.{Module}` namespaces, compiled into **separate class libraries** referenced by a thin *Composition Root* (Web / gRPC Host).\n...\n6. **Dependency Inversion through Internal DI Container**\n   All external dependencies are injected via `IServiceCollection` extensions located in each module's `Infrastructure` layer.\n```\n\n### 2. Event-Driven Monitoring Pattern (ADR-002)\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/002-event-driven-monitoring.md\n// Lines: 39-46\n\nWe will implement a lightweight, in-process **Event Bus** backed by\n`System.Threading.Channels` for default deployments, with adapters that\nproxy to external brokers (Kafka / Azure Event Hubs) for scale-out\nenvironments. All monitoring signals will be published as immutable\ndomain events implementing `IModelEvent`. Down-stream subscribers may\nreact synchronously or asynchronously (e.g., stream to the dashboard,\nwrite to the Feature Store, or trigger auto-retraining).\n```\n\n### 3. ServingController - Prediction Tracking\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Api/Controllers/ServingController.cs\n// Lines: 88-104\n\n// 2) Run inference.\nvar output = await _inferenceService.PredictAsync(\n    manifest,\n    request.Features,\n    ct);\n\n// 3) Persist prediction event for audit / feedback loop.\nvar predictionId = Guid.NewGuid().ToString(\"N\");\nawait _trackingService.TrackPredictionAsync(\n    new PredictionEvent\n    {\n        Id = predictionId,\n        ModelId = manifest.Id,\n        ModelVersion = manifest.Version,\n        TimestampUtc = DateTime.UtcNow,\n        Input = request.Features,\n        Output = output\n    }, ct);\n```\n\n### 4. DataDriftObserver - Drift Detection & Alert Publishing\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Observers/DataDriftObserver.cs\n// Lines: 132-143\n\nprivate void RaiseAlert(DataBatchEvent batch, string featureName, double psi)\n{\n    var alert = new AlertMessage(\n        title: \"Data drift detected\",\n        body: $\"PSI={psi:F4} exceeded threshold for feature '{featureName}' in experiment {batch.ExperimentId}.\",\n        severity: AlertSeverity.Warning,\n        source: nameof(DataDriftObserver));\n\n    _alertService.Publish(alert);\n\n    _logger.LogWarning(\"Data drift detected (PSI={PSI:F4}) for feature '{Feature}' in ExperimentId={ExperimentId}.\",\n        psi, featureName, batch.ExperimentId);\n}\n```\n\n### 6. AutomatedRetrainingTrigger - Subscribes to IModelMonitor\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Pipeline/Triggers/AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs\n// Lines: 24-61\n\npublic sealed class AutomatedRetrainingTrigger : IObserver<ModelDriftReport>, IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cts             = new();\n    private readonly IEventLogger            _logger;\n    private readonly IModelTrainingOrchestrator _orchestrator;\n    private readonly IExperimentTracker      _tracker;\n    private readonly IModelRegistry          _registry;\n    ...\n\n    public AutomatedRetrainingTrigger(\n        IModelMonitor                monitor,\n        IModelTrainingOrchestrator   orchestrator,\n        IExperimentTracker           tracker,\n        IModelRegistry               registry,\n        IEventLogger                 logger,\n        TimeSpan?                    debounceWindow = null,\n        TimeSpan?                    pollInterval   = null)\n    {\n        ...\n        // Subscribe to the monitor stream.\n        monitor.Subscribe(this);\n        _ = Task.Run(ProcessInboundQueueAsync, _cts.Token);\n    }\n\n    public void OnNext(ModelDriftReport value)\n    {\n        _inboundQueue.Enqueue(value);\n    }\n```\n\n### 7. ModelServingSubject - Observer Pattern Implementation\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Subjects/ModelServingSubject.cs\n// Lines: 27-58\n\npublic sealed class ModelServingSubject : IModelServingSubject, IObservable<ServingEventBase>, IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<IObserver<ServingEventBase>, byte> _observers;\n    private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cancellationTokenSource;\n    private bool _disposed;\n\n    public ModelServingSubject()\n    {\n        _observers = new ConcurrentDictionary<IObserver<ServingEventBase>, byte>();\n        _cancellationTokenSource = new CancellationTokenSource();\n    }\n\n    public IDisposable Subscribe(IObserver<ServingEventBase> observer)\n    {\n        if (observer == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(observer));\n\n        _observers.TryAdd(observer, 0);\n        return new Unsubscriber(_observers, observer);\n    }\n```\n\n### 8. IMessageBus - Core Abstraction\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Core/Interfaces/Services/IMessageBus.cs\n// Lines: 105-119\n\npublic interface IMessageBus\n{\n    Task PublishAsync<TEvent>(\n        TEvent @event,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TEvent : IDomainEvent;\n\n    Task SendAsync<TCommand>(\n        TCommand command,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TCommand : ICommand;\n\n    IDisposable Subscribe<TEvent>(\n        Func<TEvent, CancellationToken, Task> handler,\n        SubscriptionOptions? options = null,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TEvent : IDomainEvent;\n```\n\n### 11. docker-compose.yml - RabbitMQ Service\n\n```yaml\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docker-compose.yml\n// Lines: 180-200\n\n# RabbitMQ: Asynchronous orchestration\nrabbitmq:\n  image: rabbitmq:3.11-management\n  container_name: canvascraft-rabbitmq\n  restart: unless-stopped\n  environment:\n    RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: \"canvas\"\n    RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: \"secret\"\n  volumes:\n    - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq\n  ports:\n    - \"5672:5672\"     # AMQP\n    - \"15672:15672\"   # Management UI\n  networks:\n    - ml_net\n```\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### 1. Current State: Modular Monolith with Event-Driven Monitoring\n\nThe CanvasCraft ML Studio is architected as a **C# .NET 8 modular monolith** with clearly defined module boundaries. The system employs an **event-driven architecture** for monitoring using the **Observer Pattern**.\n\n#### Current Data Flow:\n\n1. **Prediction Request** \u2192 `ServingController` receives prediction requests at `/api/serve/{modelName}/predict`\n\n2. **Inference Execution** \u2192 The controller calls `IInferenceService.PredictAsync()` to execute the model\n\n3. **Event Publication** \u2192 After prediction, `IExperimentTrackingService.TrackPredictionAsync()` is called to persist a `PredictionEvent` for audit/feedback loop\n\n4. **Monitoring Subscription** \u2192 The `ModelServingSubject` (implementing `IObservable<ServingEventBase>`) acts as the central hub for serving events. Observers like `DataDriftObserver` and `PerformanceFadeObserver` subscribe to this subject\n\n5. **Drift Detection** \u2192 `DataDriftObserver` computes PSI (Population Stability Index) against baseline distributions. When drift exceeds thresholds, it calls `IAlertService.Publish()` to raise alerts\n\n6. **Retraining Trigger** \u2192 `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` subscribes to `IModelMonitor` (which publishes `ModelDriftReport` events). When `ShouldRetrain` threshold is met, it orchestrates retraining via `IModelTrainingOrchestrator`\n\n7. **Model Registration** \u2192 New model artifacts are registered via `IModelRegistry.RegisterNewModelAsync()`\n\n#### Key Components:\n\n| Component | Location | Role |\n|-----------|----------|------|\n| `ServingController` | CanvasCraft.Api | API entry point, publishes prediction events |\n| `ModelServingSubject` | CanvasCraft.Monitoring | Observer pattern subject for serving events |\n| `DataDriftObserver` | CanvasCraft.Monitoring | PSI-based drift detection |\n| `PerformanceFadeObserver` | CanvasCraft.Monitoring | Performance degradation detection |\n| `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` | CanvasCraft.Pipeline | Subscribes to drift events, triggers retraining |\n| `RabbitMqService` | CanvasCraft.Infrastructure | Message broker implementation |\n| `IMessageBus` | CanvasCraft.Core | Abstraction for publish/subscribe |\n\n#### Current In-Process Architecture:\n- All modules run in the **same process** (single deployment unit)\n- Communication uses **in-memory** channels and the Observer pattern\n- DI registration happens in `Startup.cs` (composition root)\n- The `DriftDetectionObserver` is registered as a singleton\n\n---\n\n### 2. Proposed Microservice Architecture\n\n#### 2.a. Communication Strategy\n\n**Recommendation: Asynchronous Communication via RabbitMQ**\n\n**Justification:**\n1. **ADR-002 establishes event-driven patterns**: The architecture already uses `IEventBus` and `IMessageBus` abstractions with RabbitMQ adapters for scale-out\n2. **Existing RabbitMQ infrastructure**: `docker-compose.yml` already includes RabbitMQ (port 5672/15672)\n3. **Loose coupling**: Asynchronous messaging maintains the decoupling principle from ADR-001 (\"producers/consumers remain oblivious of each other\")\n4. **Independent scaling**: The monitoring service can scale independently without blocking the main API\n\n**Pattern:**\n- Use **Topic Exchange** in RabbitMQ for event routing\n- `CanvasCraft.Api` publishes `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent` to exchange\n- `MonitoringService` subscribes to prediction events queue\n- `MonitoringService` publishes `DriftDetectedEvent`/`RetrainingRequiredEvent` back to RabbitMQ\n- `CanvasCraft.Pipeline` subscribes to retraining events\n\n#### 2.b. Data Flow (Proposed)\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Flow:**\n\n1. **`CanvasCraft.Api`** publishes `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent` to RabbitMQ `predictions.exchange` with routing key `model.prediction.queried`\n\n2. **`MonitoringService`** (new microservice) subscribes to `predictions.queue` bound to `predictions.exchange`\n\n3. **`MonitoringService`** processes events through `DataDriftObserver` and `PerformanceFadeObserver`\n\n4. Upon detecting drift, **`MonitoringService`** publishes:\n   - `DriftDetectedEvent` to `monitoring.exchange` with routing key `model.drift.detected`\n   - `RetrainingRequiredEvent` to `retraining.exchange` with routing key `model.retrain.required`\n\n5. **`AutomatedRetrainingTrigger`** in `CanvasCraft.Pipeline` subscribes to `retraining.queue` and initiates retraining\n\n---\n\n### 3. The refactoring maintains loose coupling through asynchronous message-based communication.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` (Observers: DataDriftObserver, PerformanceFadeObserver; Subjects: ModelServingSubject)\n  - `CanvasCraft.Api/Startup.cs` (DI registrations to remove)\n  - `CanvasCraft.Pipeline/Triggers/AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs` (subscription source change)\n  - `CanvasCraft.Infrastructure/Services/RabbitMqService.cs` (existing message bus)\n  - `docker-compose.yml` (new service definition)\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: **Event-Driven Architecture** using **Observer Pattern** with **RabbitMQ** as the message broker. The new architecture follows **microservice principles** with independent deployment, asynchronous communication, and loose coupling via publish/subscribe messaging.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Create a shared contracts library (`CanvasCraft.Contracts`) to define event schemas\n  2. Use topic exchange in RabbitMQ for flexible routing (e.g., `model.prediction.*`, `model.drift.*`)\n  3. Implement idempotent event handlers in the monitoring service (events may be delivered at-least-once)\n  4. Add correlation IDs to all events for distributed tracing (already present in `IMonitoringEvent.CorrelationId`)\n  5. Configure dead-letter queues for failed message handling\n  6. Update Prometheus scrape config to include the new monitoring-service endpoint\n  7. Consider implementing a circuit breaker (Polly already used in RabbitMqService) for resilience\n",

Modular Monolith Architecture Decision (ADR-001)\n\n```markdown\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/001-modular-monolith-architecture.md\n// Lines: 29-52\n\nGiven current **team size**, the **need for synchronous cross-module transactions** (e.g., dataset \u2194 feature store \u2194 model registry), and the **desire to postpone DevOps overhead** until usage patterns stabilize, we choose the **Modular Monolith**.\n\n## 2. Decision\n\nWe will build CanvasCraft ML Studio as a **C# 8/9, .NET 8** modular monolith with the following rules:\n\n1. **Single Deployment Unit**\n   A single Docker container / process hosts all modules (Train, Serve, Monitor, UX, etc.).\n2. **Explicit Module Boundaries**\n   Modules are organized under `/src/{BoundedContext}.{Module}` namespaces, compiled into **separate class libraries** referenced by a thin *Composition Root* (Web / gRPC Host).\n...\n6. **Dependency Inversion through Internal DI Container**\n   All external dependencies are injected via `IServiceCollection` extensions located in each module's `Infrastructure` layer.\n```\n\n### 2. Event-Driven Monitoring Pattern (ADR-002)\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/002-event-driven-monitoring.md\n// Lines: 39-46\n\nWe will implement a lightweight, in-process **Event Bus** backed by\n`System.Threading.Channels` for default deployments, with adapters that\nproxy to external brokers (Kafka / Azure Event Hubs) for scale-out\nenvironments. All monitoring signals will be published as immutable\ndomain events implementing `IModelEvent`. Down-stream subscribers may\nreact synchronously or asynchronously (e.g., stream to the dashboard,\nwrite to the Feature Store, or trigger auto-retraining).\n```\n\n### 3. ServingController - Prediction Tracking\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Api/Controllers/ServingController.cs\n// Lines: 88-104\n\n// 2) Run inference.\nvar output = await _inferenceService.PredictAsync(\n    manifest,\n    request.Features,\n    ct);\n\n// 3) Persist prediction event for audit / feedback loop.\nvar predictionId = Guid.NewGuid().ToString(\"N\");\nawait _trackingService.TrackPredictionAsync(\n    new PredictionEvent\n    {\n        Id = predictionId,\n        ModelId = manifest.Id,\n        ModelVersion = manifest.Version,\n        TimestampUtc = DateTime.UtcNow,\n        Input = request.Features,\n        Output = output\n    }, ct);\n```\n\n### 4. ModelPredictionQueriedEvent - Monitoring Event Contract\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Events/ModelPredictionQueriedEvent.cs\n// Lines: 11-22\n\npublic interface IMonitoringEvent\n{\n    /// <summary>Unique identifier for the event instance.</summary>\n    Guid EventId { get; }\n\n    /// <summary>UTC timestamp indicating when the event occurred.</summary>\n    DateTimeOffset Timestamp { get; }\n}\n```\n\n### 5. DataDriftObserver - Drift Detection & Alert Publishing\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Observers/DataDriftObserver.cs\n// Lines: 132-143\n\nprivate void RaiseAlert(DataBatchEvent batch, string featureName, double psi)\n{\n    var alert = new AlertMessage(\n        title: \"Data drift detected\",\n        body: $\"PSI={psi:F4} exceeded threshold for feature '{featureName}' in experiment {batch.ExperimentId}.\",\n        severity: AlertSeverity.Warning,\n        source: nameof(DataDriftObserver));\n\n    _alertService.Publish(alert);\n\n    _logger.LogWarning(\"Data drift detected (PSI={PSI:F4}) for feature '{Feature}' in ExperimentId={ExperimentId}.\",\n        psi, featureName, batch.ExperimentId);\n}\n```\n\n### 6. AutomatedRetrainingTrigger - Subscribes to IModelMonitor\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Pipeline/Triggers/AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs\n// Lines: 24-61\n\npublic sealed class AutomatedRetrainingTrigger : IObserver<ModelDriftReport>, IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cts             = new();\n    private readonly IEventLogger            _logger;\n    private readonly IModelTrainingOrchestrator _orchestrator;\n    private readonly IExperimentTracker      _tracker;\n    private readonly IModelRegistry          _registry;\n    ...\n\n    public AutomatedRetrainingTrigger(\n        IModelMonitor                monitor,\n        IModelTrainingOrchestrator   orchestrator,\n        IExperimentTracker           tracker,\n        IModelRegistry               registry,\n        IEventLogger                 logger,\n        TimeSpan?                    debounceWindow = null,\n        TimeSpan?                    pollInterval   = null)\n    {\n        ...\n        // Subscribe to the monitor stream.\n        monitor.Subscribe(this);\n        _ = Task.Run(ProcessInboundQueueAsync, _cts.Token);\n    }\n\n    public void OnNext(ModelDriftReport value)\n    {\n        _inboundQueue.Enqueue(value);\n    }\n```\n\n### 7. ModelServingSubject - Observer Pattern Implementation\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Subjects/ModelServingSubject.cs\n// Lines: 27-58\n\npublic sealed class ModelServingSubject : IModelServingSubject, IObservable<ServingEventBase>, IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<IObserver<ServingEventBase>, byte> _observers;\n    private readonly CancellationTokenSource _cancellationTokenSource;\n    private bool _disposed;\n\n    public ModelServingSubject()\n    {\n        _observers = new ConcurrentDictionary<IObserver<ServingEventBase>, byte>();\n        _cancellationTokenSource = new CancellationTokenSource();\n    }\n\n    public IDisposable Subscribe(IObserver<ServingEventBase> observer)\n    {\n        if (observer == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(observer));\n\n        _observers.TryAdd(observer, 0);\n        return new Unsubscriber(_observers, observer);\n    }\n```\n\n### 8. Startup.cs - DI Registration including Observer\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Api/Startup.cs\n// Lines: 99-104\n\n// MLOps pipeline orchestrator (Pipeline Pattern)\nservices.AddScoped<IMLopsPipeline, MlOpsPipeline>();\n\n// Observer Pattern \u2013 notify when model performance drifts\nservices.AddSingleton<IModelPerformanceObserver, DriftDetectionObserver>();\n```\n\n### 9. RabbitMqService - Message Bus Implementation\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Infrastructure/Services/RabbitMqService.cs\n// Lines: 54-68\n\npublic interface IRabbitMqService : IDisposable\n{\n    Task PublishAsync<TMessage>(\n        TMessage message,\n        string routingKey,\n        string? exchange = null,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n\n    Task<IDisposable> SubscribeAsync<TMessage>(\n        string queue,\n        Func<TMessage, Task> onMessageAsync,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n\n    bool IsHealthy { get; }\n}\n```\n\n### 10. IMessageBus - Core Abstraction\n\n```csharp\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Core/Interfaces/Services/IMessageBus.cs\n// Lines: 105-119\n\npublic interface IMessageBus\n{\n    Task PublishAsync<TEvent>(\n        TEvent @event,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TEvent : IDomainEvent;\n\n    Task SendAsync<TCommand>(\n        TCommand command,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TCommand : ICommand;\n\n    IDisposable Subscribe<TEvent>(\n        Func<TEvent, CancellationToken, Task> handler,\n        SubscriptionOptions? options = null,\n        CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        where TEvent : IDomainEvent;\n```\n\n### 11. docker-compose.yml - RabbitMQ Service\n\n```yaml\n// File: /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docker-compose.yml\n// Lines: 180-200\n\n# RabbitMQ: Asynchronous orchestration\nrabbitmq:\n  image: rabbitmq:3.11-management\n  container_name: canvascraft-rabbitmq\n  restart: unless-stopped\n  environment:\n    RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: \"canvas\"\n    RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: \"secret\"\n  volumes:\n    - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq\n  ports:\n    - \"5672:5672\"     # AMQP\n    - \"15672:15672\"   # Management UI\n  networks:\n    - ml_net\n```\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### 1. Current State: Modular Monolith with Event-Driven Monitoring\n\nThe CanvasCraft ML Studio is architected as a **C# .NET 8 modular monolith** with clearly defined module boundaries. The system employs an **event-driven architecture** for monitoring using the **Observer Pattern**.\n\n#### Current Data Flow:\n\n1. **Prediction Request** \u2192 `ServingController` receives prediction requests at `/api/serve/{modelName}/predict`\n\n2. **Inference Execution** \u2192 The controller calls `IInferenceService.PredictAsync()` to execute the model\n\n3. **Event Publication** \u2192 After prediction, `IExperimentTrackingService.TrackPredictionAsync()` is called to persist a `PredictionEvent` for audit/feedback loop\n\n4. **Monitoring Subscription** \u2192 The `ModelServingSubject` (implementing `IObservable<ServingEventBase>`) acts as the central hub for serving events. Observers like `DataDriftObserver` and `PerformanceFadeObserver` subscribe to this subject\n\n5. **Drift Detection** \u2192 `DataDriftObserver` computes PSI (Population Stability Index) against baseline distributions. When drift exceeds thresholds, it calls `IAlertService.Publish()` to raise alerts\n\n6. **Retraining Trigger** \u2192 `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` subscribes to `IModelMonitor` (which publishes `ModelDriftReport` events). When `ShouldRetrain` threshold is met, it orchestrates retraining via `IModelTrainingOrchestrator`\n\n7. **Model Registration** \u2192 New model artifacts are registered via `IModelRegistry.RegisterNewModelAsync()`\n\n#### Key Components:\n\n| Component | Location | Role |\n|-----------|----------|------|\n| `ServingController` | CanvasCraft.Api | API entry point, publishes prediction events |\n| `ModelServingSubject` | CanvasCraft.Monitoring | Observer pattern subject for serving events |\n| `DataDriftObserver` | CanvasCraft.Monitoring | PSI-based drift detection |\n| `PerformanceFadeObserver` | CanvasCraft.Monitoring | Performance degradation detection |\n| `AutomatedRetrainingTrigger` | CanvasCraft.Pipeline | Subscribes to drift events, triggers retraining |\n| `RabbitMqService` | CanvasCraft.Infrastructure | Message broker implementation |\n| `IMessageBus` | CanvasCraft.Core | Abstraction for publish/subscribe |\n\n#### Current In-Process Architecture:\n- All modules run in the **same process** (single deployment unit)\n- Communication uses **in-memory** channels and the Observer pattern\n- DI registration happens in `Startup.cs` (composition root)\n- The `DriftDetectionObserver` is registered as a singleton\n\n---\n\n### 2. Proposed Microservice Architecture\n\n#### 2.a. Communication Strategy\n\n**Recommendation: Asynchronous Communication via RabbitMQ**\n\n**Justification:**\n1. **ADR-002 establishes event-driven patterns**: The architecture already uses `IEventBus` and `IMessageBus` abstractions with RabbitMQ adapters for scale-out\n2. **Existing RabbitMQ infrastructure**: `docker-compose.yml` already includes RabbitMQ (port 5672/15672)\n3. **Loose coupling**: Asynchronous messaging maintains the decoupling principle from ADR-001 (\"producers/consumers remain oblivious of each other\")\n4. **Independent scaling**: The monitoring service can scale independently without blocking the main API\n\n**Pattern:**\n- Use **Topic Exchange** in RabbitMQ for event routing\n- `CanvasCraft.Api` publishes `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent` to exchange\n- `MonitoringService` subscribes to prediction events queue\n- `MonitoringService` publishes `DriftDetectedEvent`/`RetrainingRequiredEvent` back to RabbitMQ\n- `CanvasCraft.Pipeline` subscribes to retraining events\n\n#### 2.b. Data Flow (Proposed)\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502 Flow:**\n\n1. **`CanvasCraft.Api`** publishes `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent` to RabbitMQ `predictions.exchange` with routing key `model.prediction.queried`\n\n2. **`MonitoringService`** (new microservice) subscribes to `predictions.queue` bound to `predictions.exchange`\n\n3. **`MonitoringService`** processes events through `DataDriftObserver` and `PerformanceFadeObserver`\n\n4. Upon detecting drift, **`MonitoringService`** publishes:\n   - `DriftDetectedEvent` to `monitoring.exchange` with routing key `model.drift.detected`\n   - `RetrainingRequiredEvent` to `retraining.exchange` with routing key `model.retrain.required`\n\n5. **`AutomatedRetrainingTrigger`** in `CanvasCraft.Pipeline` subscribes to `retraining.queue` and initiates retraining\n\n---\n\n### 3. Implementation & Refactoring Plan\n\n#### 3.a. Code Changes Required\n\n##### Files to Modify in `CanvasCraft.Api`:\n\n| File | Changes Required |\n|------|------------------|\n| `src/CanvasCraft.Api/Startup.cs` | **Remove** DI registration for `IModelPerformanceObserver, DriftDetectionObserver`. Remove any direct monitoring module dependencies. Add `IRabbitMqService` registration for event publishing. |\n| `src/CanvasCraft.Api/Controllers/ServingController.cs` | **Modify** to publish `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent` via `IMessageBus.PublishAsync()` instead of calling tracking service directly |\n| `src/CanvasCraft.Api/Controllers/MonitoringController.cs` | **Modify** to proxy requests to the new `MonitoringService` via HTTP/gRPC, or consume from shared RabbitMQ queues for SSE streaming |\n\n##### Files to Modify in `CanvasCraft.Pipeline`:\n\n| File | Changes Required |\n|------|------------------|\n| `src/CanvasCraft.Pipeline/Triggers/AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs` | **Modify** constructor to accept `IMessageBus` instead of `IModelMonitor`. Subscribe to `RetrainingRequiredEvent` from RabbitMQ instead of in-process observable |\n\n##### Project References to Remove:\n\n| Project | Remove Reference To |\n|---------|---------------------|\n| `CanvasCraft.Api` | `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` (direct reference) |\n| `CanvasCraft.Pipeline` | `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` (if directly referenced for observer types) |\n\n##### Shared Contracts to Extract:\n\nCreate a new shared library `CanvasCraft.Contracts` containing:\n- `ModelPredictionQueriedEvent`\n- `DriftDetectedEvent`\n- `RetrainingRequiredEvent`\n- `IMonitoringEvent` interface\n\nBoth the main application and the new microservice will reference this contracts assembly.\n\n#### 3.b. New Components: MonitoringService Structure\n\n```\nMonitoringService/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 src/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 MonitoringService/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Program.cs                    # .NET 8 Minimal API host\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 appsettings.json              # RabbitMQ, Redis connection strings\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Dockerfile                    # Container image definition\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Consumers/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 PredictionEventConsumer.cs # RabbitMQ consumer for predictions\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Observers/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 DataDriftObserver.cs      # Extracted from CanvasCraft.Monitoring\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 PerformanceFadeObserver.cs\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Publishers/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 DriftEventPublisher.cs    # Publishes DriftDetectedEvent\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Services/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 MonitoringService.cs      # Orchestrates drift detection\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 FeatureStatisticsService.cs # Access to baseline statistics\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 HealthChecks/\n\u2502   \u2502       \u2514\u2500\u2500 RabbitMqHealthCheck.cs\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 MonitoringService.csproj\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 tests/\n    \u2514\u2500\u2500 MonitoringService.Tests/\n```\n\n**API Contract (Optional REST API for ad-hoc queries):**\n\n```csharp\n// GET /api/monitoring/health\n// GET /api/monitoring/models/{modelId}/drift-status\n// POST /api/monitoring/models/{modelId}/drift-check\n```\n\n**Message Consumer Contract:**\n\n```csharp\npublic class PredictionEventConsumer : BackgroundService\n{\n    private readonly IRabbitMqService _rabbitMq;\n    private readonly IMonitoringService _monitoringService;\n\n    protected override async Task ExecuteAsync(CancellationToken stoppingToken)\n    {\n        await _rabbitMq.SubscribeAsync<ModelPredictionQueriedEvent>(\n            \"predictions.queue\",\n            async msg => await _monitoringService.ProcessPredictionAsync(msg),\n            stoppingToken);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n#### 3.c. Deployment: docker-compose.yml Changes\n\nAdd the following service definition to `docker-compose.yml`:\n\n```yaml\n# --------------------------------------------------\n# Monitoring Service: Data Drift & Performance Detection\n# --------------------------------------------------\nmonitoring-service:\n  build:\n    context: ./src/MonitoringService\n    dockerfile: Dockerfile\n  container_name: canvascraft-monitoring-service\n  environment:\n    ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT: \"Production\"\n    RABBITMQ__HOST: \"rabbitmq\"\n    RABBITMQ__PORT: \"5672\"\n    RABBITMQ__USERNAME: \"canvas\"\n    RABBITMQ__PASSWORD: \"secret\"\n    RABBITMQ__VIRTUAL_HOST: \"/\"\n    CONNECTIONSTRINGS__Redis: \"redis:6379\"\n    CONNECTIONSTRINGS__Postgres: \"Host=postgres;Port=5432;Database=canvascraft;Username=canvas;Password=secret\"\n    FEATURE_STORE__ENDPOINT: \"http://minio:9000\"\n  depends_on:\n    - rabbitmq\n    - redis\n    - postgres\n  ports:\n    - \"5010:80\"   # Optional REST API port\n  networks:\n    - ml_net\n  restart: unless-stopped\n  healthcheck:\n    test: [\"CMD\", \"curl\", \"-f\", \"http://localhost:80/health\"]\n    interval: 30s\n    timeout: 10s\n    retries: 3\n```\n\n**Update API service to depend on monitoring-service:**\n\n```yaml\napi:\n  ...\n  depends_on:\n    - postgres\n    - redis\n    - rabbitmq\n    - minio\n    - monitoring-service  # Optional: if API needs to health-check monitoring\n```\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\n- **Primary finding**: The CanvasCraft.Monitoring module can be extracted into a standalone microservice by leveraging the existing RabbitMQ infrastructure and event-driven patterns already established in ADR-002. The refactoring maintains loose coupling through asynchronous message-based communication.\n\n- **Key components**:\n  - `CanvasCraft.Monitoring` (Observers: DataDriftObserver, PerformanceFadeObserver; Subjects: ModelServingSubject)\n  - `CanvasCraft.Api/Startup.cs` (DI registrations to remove)\n  - `CanvasCraft.Pipeline/Triggers/AutomatedRetrainingTrigger.cs` (subscription source change)\n  - `CanvasCraft.Infrastructure/Services/RabbitMqService.cs` (existing message bus)\n  - `docker-compose.yml` (new service definition)\n\n- **Architectural pattern**: **Event-Driven Architecture** using **Observer Pattern** with **RabbitMQ** as the message broker. The new architecture follows **microservice principles** with independent deployment, asynchronous communication, and loose coupling via publish/subscribe messaging.\n\n- **Recommendations**:\n  1. Create a shared contracts library (`CanvasCraft.Contracts`) to define event schemas\n  2. Use topic exchange in RabbitMQ for flexible routing (e.g., `model.prediction.*`, `model.drift.*`)\n  3. Implement idempotent event handlers in the monitoring service (events may be delivered at-least-once)\n  4. Add correlation IDs to all events for distributed tracing (already present in `IMonitoringEvent.CorrelationId`)\n  5. Configure dead-letter queues for failed message handling\n  6. Update Prometheus scrape config to include the new monitoring-service endpoint\n  7. Consider implementing a circuit breaker (Polly already used in RabbitMqService) for resilience\n",

# Solution: csharp_ml_training_expert_087_architectural_understanding_expert_01

## Key Files Identified

### Architecture Decision Records (ADRs)
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/001-modular-monolith-architecture.md - Establishes modular monolith as the chosen architecture, describes module boundaries and composition root pattern
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/docs/architecture/adr/002-event-driven-monitoring.md - Documents event-driven architecture for monitoring using Observer pattern and event bus

### Monitoring Module
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Events/ModelPredictionQueriedEvent.cs - Event raised when predictions are queried, contains monitoring event contract (IMonitoringEvent)
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Observers/IModelObserver.cs - Observer interface following IObserver<T> pattern with async support (IModelObserver)
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Observers/DataDriftObserver.cs - Computes data drift (PSI) against baseline training distribution, raises alerts via IAlertService
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Observers/PerformanceFadeObserver.cs - Detects performance degradation using sliding window metrics
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Subjects/ModelServingSubject.cs - Central hub implementing IObservable<ServingEventBase> for serving events
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Monitoring/Subjects/IModelSubject.cs - Subject interface for the Observer pattern

### API Layer
- /app/project/CanvasCraftMLStudio/src/CanvasCraft.Api/Controllers/ServingController.cs - REST controller for model serving, tracks predictions via IExperimentTrackingService
